								<div class="viewport-content">
									<div class="row">
										<div class="column column-copy large-centered large-12">
											<h3 class="ps-headline typography-ps-headline">
												<span class="gradient-wrapper" data-gradient-headline>All 48MP rear&nbsp;cameras.<br /> An evolution in&nbsp;resolution.</span>
											</h3>
											<p class="ps-header-copy typography-ps-body large-8 medium-10 small-12 large-centered">iPhone&nbsp;17 has a 48MP Fusion&nbsp;Main camera with a 2x optical-quality telephoto, and a <strong>48MP Fusion&nbsp;Ultra&nbsp;Wide camera with 4x the resolution</strong> of the Ultra&nbsp;Wide camera on iPhone&nbsp;16. And now Ultra Wide photos are 24MP by default, the perfect file size for high&#x2011;quality storing and sharing. So youll get stunning, super-high-resolution shots &nbsp;up close or far away, indoors and out, in conditions that go from bright to low light. And at 256GB, it has <strong>double the starting storage</strong> of the previous model.<sup data-footnote="numbered-available-space" class="footnote footnote-number"><a href="#footnote-10" aria-label="Footnote 7" data-modal-close>7</a></sup> So you can capture to your hearts content  and beyond.</p>
										</div>

						<div class="ps-header-copy typography-ps-body ric-large-6 ric-large-offset-1 ric-medium-8 ric-medium-offset-2 ric-small-12 ric-small-offset-0">The A19&nbsp;chip <strong>powers everything you do on iPhone</strong>, including Apple&nbsp;Intelligence features like Live&nbsp;Translation and Image&nbsp;Playground, and ProMotion for playing advanced AAA games. And with <strong>all-day battery life</strong>, you can work, watch, and wander with no worries. If you need a quick top-up, just <strong>10 minutes of charge gives you up to 8 hours of video playback</strong> with a high-wattage adapter.<sup data-footnote="numbered-high-wattage-adapter" class="footnote footnote-number"><a href="#footnote-12" aria-label="Footnote 9" data-modal-close>9</a></sup></div>

			<h2 class="ac-gf-label" id="ac-gf-label">Apple Footer</h2>
			<section class="ac-gf-sosumi" data-nosnippet aria-label="Footnotes">
				



























				<ul>
					<li id="footnote-1" data-footnote="starred-monthly-pricing" data-toggle-footnote="acmi"><small>*</small> Pricing for iPhone&nbsp;17 includes a $30 connectivity discount that requires carrier activation with AT&amp;T, Boost Mobile, T-Mobile, or Verizon. Financing available to qualified customers, subject to credit approval and credit limit, and requires you to select Citizens One Apple iPhone Payments or Apple&nbsp;Card Monthly&nbsp;Installments (ACMI) as your payment type at checkout at Apple. In order to buy an iPhone with ACMI, you must select one of the following carriers (but you cannot use a prepaid carrier plan): AT&amp;T, Boost Mobile, T-Mobile, or Verizon. An iPhone purchased with ACMI is always unlocked, so you can switch carriers at any time, subject to your carriers terms. Taxes and shipping on items purchased using ACMI are subject to your cards variable APR, not the ACMI 0% APR. ACMI is not available for purchases made at special storefronts or when using such special discounts in-store at Apple, except ACMI is available at the Education storefront and with the Education discount. The last months payment for each product will be the products purchase price, less all other payments at the monthly payment amount. ACMI is subject to change at any time for any reason, including but not limited to installment term lengths and eligible products. See the <a href="https://www.goldmansachs.com/terms-and-conditions/Apple-Card-Customer-Agreement.pdf" rel="nofollow">Apple&nbsp;Card Customer Agreement</a> for more information about ACMI. Additional Citizens One Apple iPhone Payments terms are&nbsp;<a href="/legal/sales-support/iphoneinstallments_us/">here</a>.</li>
					<li id="footnote-2" data-footnote="starred-trade-in-tile"><small>**</small> Trade&#x2011;in values will vary based on the condition, year, and configuration of your eligible trade&#x2011;in device. Not all devices are eligible for credit. You must be at least the age of majority to be eligible to trade in for credit or for an Apple&nbsp;Gift&nbsp;Card. Trade&#x2011;in value may be applied toward qualifying new device purchase, or added to an Apple&nbsp;Gift&nbsp;Card. Actual value awarded is based on receipt of a qualifying device matching the description provided when estimate was made. Sales tax may be assessed on full value of a new device purchase. In&#x2011;store trade&#x2011;in requires presentation of a valid photo ID (local law may require saving this information). Offer may not be available in all stores, and may vary between in&#x2011;store and online trade&#x2011;in. Some stores may have additional requirements. Apple or its trade&#x2011;in partners reserve the right to refuse, cancel, or limit quantity of any trade&#x2011;in transaction for any reason. More details are available from Apples trade&#x2011;in partner for trade&#x2011;in and recycling of eligible devices. Restrictions and limitations may&nbsp;apply.</li>
					<li id="footnote-3" data-footnote="starred-acmi" data-toggle-footnote="acmi"><small>***</small>
						Apple Card Monthly Installments (ACMI) is a 0% APR payment option that is only available if you select it at checkout in the U.S. for eligible products purchased at Apple Store locations, <a href="/">apple.com</a>, the Apple Store app, or by calling 1&#8209;800&#8209;MY&#8209;APPLE, and is subject to credit approval and credit limit. See <a href="https://support.apple.com/102730?cid=general-phone-marcom-08062025">here</a> for more information about eligible products. Existing customers: See your Customer Agreement for your variable APR. As of January 1, 2026, the variable APR on new Apple Card accounts ranges from 17.49% to 27.74%. You must elect to use ACMI at checkout. If you buy an ACMI&#8209;eligible product with a one-time payment on Apple Card at checkout, that purchase is subject to your Apple Cards variable APR, not the ACMI 0% APR. Taxes and shipping on items purchased using ACMI are subject to your Apple Cards variable APR, not the ACMI 0% APR. In order to buy an iPhone with ACMI, you must select one of the following carriers (prepaid carrier plans are not supported): AT&T, Boost Mobile, T&#8209;Mobile, or Verizon. An iPhone purchased with ACMI is always unlocked, so you can switch carriers at any time, subject to your carriers terms. ACMI is not available for purchases made at the following special storefronts or when using these discounts in-store at Apple: Apple Employee Purchase Plan; participating corporate Employee Purchase Programs; Apple at Work for small businesses; Government and Veterans and Military Purchase Programs; or on refurbished devices. The last months payment for each product will be the products purchase price, less all other payments at the monthly payment amount. ACMI is subject to change at any time for any reason, including but not limited to installment term lengths and eligible products. See the <a href="https://www.goldmansachs.com/terms-and-conditions/Apple-Card-Customer-Agreement.pdf" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Apple Card Customer Agreement</a> for more information about ACMI.

<div style="padding-top: 0.8em;"><p>To access and use all Apple&nbsp;Card features and products available only to Apple&nbsp;Card users, you must add Apple&nbsp;Card to Wallet on an iPhone or iPad that supports and has the latest version of iOS or iPadOS. Apple&nbsp;Card is subject to credit approval, available only for qualifying applicants in the United States, and issued by Goldman Sachs Bank USA, Salt Lake City Branch.</p>
<p style="padding-top: 0.8em;">Apple&nbsp;Payments&nbsp;Services&nbsp;LLC, a subsidiary of Apple&nbsp;Inc., is a service provider of Goldman Sachs Bank USA for Apple&nbsp;Card and Savings accounts. Neither Apple&nbsp;Inc. nor Apple&nbsp;Payments&nbsp;Services&nbsp;LLC is a bank.</p>
<p style="padding-top: 0.8em;">All communications from Apple and Goldman Sachs Bank USA about Apple&nbsp;Card (including transactional and marketing communications) and customer service support are available in English. Certain communications about Apple&nbsp;Card can be viewed in another language depending on your device language settings. If you reside in the U.S. Virgin Islands, American Samoa, Guam, Northern Mariana Islands, or U.S. Minor Outlying Islands, please call Goldman Sachs at 877-255-5923 with questions about Apple&nbsp;Card.</p>

Actual viewable area is less.</li>

Apple apps that can be deleted use about 4.5GB of space, and you can download them back from the App&nbsp;Store.
